 unhone mujhe dhokhaa diya he
 "he has also accused Arafat's mother Nargis of harassment
 vakil ne kaha he, "agar vah apni pehali patni ko talaak dete hai to vah un par cese kar dengi
 Hence Arafat wants to be with both
 " At the same time, Nasreen has said that she did not know that Arafat is married
 unhone kaha, "jab ham baahar gaye to unke passport par anamarid likhaa hua tha
 They have cheated me
 " unhone araafaat kii maa naragis par bhi pratadit karne kaa aarope lagaaya he
 At the same time, Nasreen has said that she did not know that Arafat is married
 unhone kaha, "jab ham baahar gaye to unke passport par anamarid likhaa hua tha
 They have cheated me
 " unhone araafaat kii maa naragis par bhi pratadit karne kaa aarope lagaaya he
 Sri Krishna birth anniversary is being celebrated all over the country with great pomp and show
 desh ke adhikansh mandiron ko aakarshak tareeke se sajaayaa gaya he
 Janmashtami is also seen moving around in the markets
 raashtrapati pranab mukherjee ne deshavaasiyon ko janamashtami kii shubhakamanaayen di hai
 The President said in his message, On the occasion of Janmashtami, i congratulate and congratulate my countrymen
 unhone kaha, aaiye is shubh din khud ko raashtra kii seva main samarpit karen
 Let us concentrate on discharging our responsibilities without wishing for fruit
 sahi kaaryon kaa nishchit rup se acha parinaam aayega
 In his congratulatory message, Prime Minister Manmohan Singh said that Janmashtami is celebrated to commemorate the message of Lord Krishna in which he said that by doing deeds, do not desire fruit
 uparashtrapati hamid ansaari ne is maukey par deshavaasiyon ko hardik badhai dete hue kaha ki janmashtami kaa tyohaar hamen bhagwaan krishna ke jivan or shikshaaon kii yaad dilaataa he
 Meanwhile, Delhi's Lieutenant Governor Tejendra Khanna and Delhi Chief Minister Sheila Dixit have also congratulated the people of Delhi on the occasion of Janmashtami
 dilli main janmashtami ke avasar par sabhi pramukh mandir saje hue hai
 On the other hand, dahi-handi is celebrated on this occasion in Mumbai
 udhar, antarrashtriya shrikrishnabhaavnamrita sangh (isckon) dwaara shuukravaar kii raat shrikrishna memorial haul main bhagwaan shrikrishna janmashtami mahotsav kaa aayojan rakhaa gaya he
 Shri Krishna Kripa Dasji, President of ISKCON Patna, informed that Shri Krishna Leelamrit will be performed on this occasion
 isckon ke shraddhalu bhakton dwaara bhajan-kirthan or kai utkrisht aadhyatmik evam saanskrithik kaarykram pesh kiye jaaenge
 Complete preparations for the birth anniversary have been made at the radha-krishna and Lord Jagannath Temple at Ramjanaki Square in Patna
 mandiron ko aakarshak dhang se sajaayaa gaya he
 bhajan-kirtan and Lord Krishna's tableau are also prepared at night
 idhar, patna ke prasiddh mahavir mandir main guuruuvaar se teen divasiy pravachan kaa kaarykram chal rahaa he
 During this period, bhajan-kirtan has been going on all night
 iske alaava rajya ke baxur, mujffarpur, bhagalpur, purniya, aurangabad va munger sahit kai jilon main krishna janmotsav ko lekar taiyaariyaan antim charan main hai
 In many cities including Lucknow, grand treasures have been organized today
 utsav ko dekhte hue prashasan kii ore se bhi suraksha ke pukhta prabandh kiye gaye hai
 On the occasion of Janmashtami, along with householders, saints will also observe a fast today
 mandiron ke saath shahar main kai jagah kanhaiya kaa janmotsav manaaya jayega
 Due to doubt on Ashtami and Navami Tithi, most of the householders celebrated Janmashtami on Thursday itself
 pandit krishnakanth ne bataaya ki is baar gruhasthi or vaishnavon ko shuukravaar raat ko rohinee nakshatra nahin milegaa
 Rohini Nakshatra on Saturday 11 August at 9 am
 57 baje ke baad shuru hoga or yah ravivaar 12 agast ko 12
 Will remain till 31st
 unhone bataaya ki kai varshon baad aisa hua he ki jab shrikrishna janmashtami ke din rohinee nakshatra kaa sanyog nahin he
 The comments rajdhani lakhanu, varanasi, elahabaad, kanpur, agra or kai anya shaharon main janmashtami aaj manaayi ja rahi he
 Due to Janmashtami on Friday, preparations have been completed in all the temples and festive sites including the Reserve Police Line, Mahanagar, PAC ISKCON Temple and Banke Bihari Temple in Ahiaganj
 ek police adhikari ke mutabik janmashtami ke maukey par ehtiyaat ke taur par bheedbhad vaali jagahon par atirikt pulicekarmiyon kii tainaati kii gayi he
 President Pranab Mukherjee has greeted the countrymen on Janmashtami
 raashtrapati ne apane sandesh main kaha, janmashtami ke maukey par main apane deshavaasiyon ko badhai or shubhakamanaayen detaa hum
 He said, let us dedicate ourselves to the service of the nation on this auspicious day
 aaiye bina fal kii ichha kare, apni jimmedaariyon ke nirvahan kii ore dhyaan kendrit karen
 The right actions will definitely bring good results
 pradhanmantri manmohan singh ne apane badhai sandesh main kaha ki janmashtami bhagwaan krishna ke us sandesh ke uplakshya main manaaya jaataa he jisamen unhone kaha tha ki karm kar, fal kii ichha mat kar 
 Vice President Hamid Ansari congratulated the countrymen on the occasion and said that the Janmashtami festival reminds us of the life and teachings of Lord Krishna
 is bich dilli ke up rajyapal tejendra khanna or dilli kii mukhyamantri shila dikshit ne bhi aaj janmashtami ke maukey par dilli vaasiyon ko badhai di he
 All major temples are adorned on the occasion of Janmashtami in Delhi
 duusari ore mumbai main is avasar par dahi-handi kii dhooma machi hui he
 On the other hand, the International Sri Krishna Bhavnamritta Sangh (ISKCON) has organized the Lord Sri Krishna Janmashtami Festival on Friday night in Sri Krishna Memorial Hall
 isckon patna ke adhyaksh shrikrishna krupa dasji ne bataaya ki is maukey par shrikrishna lilamrita kii prastuti kii jaaegi
 ISKCON devotees will offer bhajan-kirtan and many excellent spiritual and cultural programs
 patna ke ramjanaki chauraahaa sthit radha-krishna or bhagwaan jagannatha mandir main janmotsav kii puri taiyaariyaan kar lee gai hai
 The temples are attractively decorated
 raat main bhajan-kirthan or bhagwaan krishna kii jhaanki kii bhi taiyaari kii gai he
 Here, a three-day discourse is going on in the famous Mahavir temple in Patna from Thursday
 is dauraan raatbhar bhajan-kirthan kaa daur chalata rahaa he
 Apart from this, preparations are in the final stages of Krishna Janmotsav in many districts including Buxar, Muzaffarpur, Bhagalpur, Purnia, Aurangabad and Munger in the state
 lakhanu sahit kai shaharon main aaj bhavy jhaakiyon kaa aayojan kiya gaya he
 In view of the celebration, strong security arrangements have also been made by the administration
 janmashtami ke maukey par grihasthon ke saath hi sadhu sant bhi aaj vrath rakhenge
 Kanhaiya's birth anniversary will be celebrated at many places in the city along with temples
 ashtami or navami tithi par sanshay ke chalate adhikansh grihasthon ne guuruuvaar ko hi janmashtami manaayi
 Pandit Krishnakant told that this time the householder and Vaishnavas will not get Rohini Nakshatra on Friday night
 rohinee nakshatra shanivaar 11 agast ko subah 9
 It will start after 57 pm and it will be 12 on Sunday 12 August
 31 baje tak rahegaa
 He told that after many years it has happened that when Rohini Nakshatra is not a coincidence on the day of Shri Krishna Janmashtami
 tippaniyan Janmashtami is being celebrated today in the capital Lucknow, Varanasi, Allahabad, Kanpur, Agra and many other cities
 shuukravaar ko janmashtami ke chalate rigerv police line, mahanagar, piesi isckon mandir or ahiyaganj sthit banke bihari ke mandir sahit tamaam mandiron or utsav sthalon main taiyaariyaan puri kar lee gayi hai
 According to a police officer, additional police personnel have been deployed at crowded places as a precaution on the occasion of Janmashtami

 ye companiyaan alag-alag kaam ke liye (internet se jude hue) ke liye alag-alag fees nahin vasuul sakati hai
 Under this, companies can neither reduce nor increase internet speed for any service
 agar net neutrality na ho to
 
 
 If net neutrality is not there, then the telecom operator will be the biggest beneficiary
 isse companiyon ko ye adhikaar mil jayega ki vah jis seva ke liye chahie, internet kii speed kam kar sakate hai
 Apart from this, they can increase the speed for a service on their own
 net neutrality na hone kii surat main telecom companiyaan alag-alag seva ke liye apane hisaab se internet kii speed dengi
 This service will become expensive if you have non-neutral nutritin, then it may be expensive for you to run whatsapp
 telecom oparator pichley kuch samay se ye baat kahati aa rahi hai ki whatsap ne unki SMS sarvice ko chaupat kar diya he
 Apart from this, now whatsapp has also brought calling facility
 isse telecom oparator ke kaarobaar par kaaphi asar pad rahaa he
 If you did not have net neutrality, then companies had the option of charging different and more charges for running whatsapp
 aise main koi bhi data pack jab aapako diya jaataa, to whatsap ke naam par aap se zyada charge vasula ja saktaa tha
 Apart from this, Net neutrality also gives the right to companies that they can block the website based on the content they want
 lekin tri ne apni sifarish main telecom operators kii maang ko darkinar karte hue net neutrality ke haq main faisla sunaaya he
 Companies have given the proposaltelicom companies have submitted a proposal to charge more than those using services like whatsapp, Viber and Skype, but TRAI rejected the proposal

 In Kanizia village of Mandar area of ranchi district of Jharkhand late last night, villagers killed five women by beating them with sticks using sticks as 'witch'
 is maamle main police ne 27 logon ko giraftaar kiya he
 Ranchi Deputy Inspector General of Police Arun Kumar said that in a heartbreaking incident at Kanijia village in Mandar area, twenty kilometers from the capital Ranchi, late last night, the villagers beat them with sticks and sticks as 'witch', aged between 32 and 50 Killed five women ruthlessly
 iske baad unki laashon ko bore main baandhakar gaanv se baahar phenk diya
 He said that after preliminary investigation, police have registered an FIR for murder against about fifty people in this case of brutal murder and 27 of them have been arrested
 is bich, mukhyamantri raghuvar das ne ghatana par kshobh vyakt karte hue kaha, 'gyaan or soochna ke is yug main is tarah kii ghatana se maanavtaa sharmasaar hoti he
 'he has asked the society to wake up and spread consciousness among people to prevent such incidents
 unhone police se is ghatana main shaamil logon ke khilaaf kathor karrwai karne ko kaha he
 On the other hand, Deputy Inspector General of Police said that the post mortem of the dead bodies has been done by the police and the reason for killing all is proved to be a stab with sticks
 unhone bataaya ki vah swayan abhi bhi mauka-e-vaardaat par hi hai, or puure ilaake main badi sankhya main police bal kii tainaati kii gai he
 The villagers also protested against the police taking possession of the corpse by reaching the village early in the morning due to superstition and they are also opposed to burying them in the village cemetery
 arun kumaar ne ghatana kaa vivaran dete hue bataaya ki kuch dinon pehle gaanv main do teen adhed umr ke logon kii agyaat kaarnon se maut ho gai jise kuch logon ne 'dian' ke prabhaav se hui maut bataakar logon main bhranti failaane kaa kaam kiya
 After this, an 18-year-old man died of jaundice in the neighborhood of the house of one of the women killed just two days ago
 police upmahanireekshak ne bataaya ki gaanv waalon ne mrit yuvak ke pados main rahane vaali ek mahila ko dian bataakar peetna shuru kar diya
 The beaten woman took the names of four other women and the villagers also took them out of their houses and started beating them with sticks, which caused the five women to die there itself
 unhone bataaya ki rajya sarkaar or khaskar mukhyamantri ne puri ghatana ko bahut gambhirtha se liya he or iske khilaaf sakht karrwai kii jaaegi
 The police are vigorously searching for the absconding accused and all are likely to be arrested by night
 tippaniyan On the other hand, the state's Urban Development Minister and Ranchi MLA CP Singh expressed deep sorrow over this incident and appealed to the people to get away from such malpractices
 unhone jan-jan main aisi kuritiyon ke khilaaf chetana laane ke kaarykram chalaane kii baat kahi
 State Women's Commission chairperson Mahua Manjhi also condemned the incident and said that she would visit the spot along with her team in two-three days and take stock of it
 unhone kaha ki is tarah kii ghatnaayen adhiktar yaa to bhranti ke kaaran athwa akeli mahilaon kii sampatti hadapney kii niyat se sajeesh ke tahat kii jaati hai
 She said that a proper women's policy is needed to prevent recurrence of such incidents
 ranchi ke police upmahanireekshak arun kumaar ne bataaya ki kal der raat rajdhani ranchi se bees kilometre dur mander ilaake main kanijia gaanv main ek dil dahala dene vaali ghatana main gaanv waalon ne 'dian' bataakar lathi-danda se peet kar 32 se 50 saal kii umr kii paanch mahilaon kii nirmam hatya kar di
 After this, their dead bodies were tied in sacks and thrown out of the village
 unhone bataaya ki police ne shuruaati jaanch ke baad nrushans hatya ke is maamle main lagbhag pachaas logon ke khilaaf hatya kii exiaar darj kii he or inamen se 27 logon ko giraftaar bhi kar liya he
 Meanwhile, Chief Minister Raghuvar Das expressed anguish over the incident, saying, 'in this age of knowledge and information, such an event shames humanity
 ' unhone samaaj se jaagane or aisi ghatnaon ko rokane ke liye logon main chetana failaane ko kaha he
 He has asked the police to take stern action against those involved in the incident
 vahiin police upmahanireekshak ne bataaya ki maare gaye logon ke shavon kaa postmortem police ne karvaa liya he or sabhi ko maare jane kaa kaaran un par lathi danda se waar hi sabit hua he
 He said that he himself is still on the scene, and a large number of police forces have been deployed throughout the area
 graminon ne andhvishwaas ke chalate sabere police ke gaanv pahunchakar laash kabje main lene kaa bhi virodh kiya or gaanv ke kabrgah main unhen dafnane kaa bhi vah virodh kar rahe hai
 Giving details of the incident, Arun Kumar said that a few days ago two-three middle-aged people died in the village due to unknown reasons, which some people said was a death due to the influence of 'witch'
 iske baad abhi do dinon pehle maari gai mahilaon main se ek ke ghar ke pados main 18 saal ke yuvak kii pilia se maut ho gai
 The Deputy Inspector General of Police said that the villagers started beating a woman living in the neighborhood of the dead youth as a witch

 He informed that the state government and especially the Chief Minister has taken the entire incident very seriously and strict action will be taken against it

 tippaniyan Though he admitted that it is difficult to distinguish between real handsets with the same IMEI numbers and fake handsets, the Department of Telecom is trying to find a solution to the problem of using illegal imeis and the same IMEI in different mobile phones

 unhone bataaya ki iemiai ke sambandh main april, 2009 main hi nirdesh jari kiye gaye the
